                                (SELECT F10003, ValStr, Ziua From Ptj_Intrari_2 WHERE '2020-05-01' <= CAST(Ziua AS date) AND CAST(Ziua AS date) <= '2020-05-31') AS source  
                                PIVOT  (MAX(ValStr) FOR Ziua IN (  [2020-05-01], [2020-05-02], [2020-05-03], [2020-05-04], [2020-05-05], [2020-05-06], [2020-05-07], [2020-05-08], [2020-05-09], [2020-05-10], [2020-05-11], [2020-05-12], [2020-05-13], [2020-05-14], [2020-05-15], [2020-05-16], [2020-05-17], [2020-05-18], [2020-05-19], [2020-05-20], [2020-05-21], [2020-05-22], [2020-05-23], [2020-05-24], [2020-05-25], [2020-05-26], [2020-05-27], [2020-05-28], [2020-05-29], [2020-05-30], [2020-05-31] )) pvt
                                ) pvt ON X.F10003=pvt.F10003
                                LEFT JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=X.F10003 
                                LEFT JOIN F1001 B ON A.F10003=B.F10003 
                                LEFT JOIN (SELECT R.F10003, MIN(R.Ziua) AS ZiuaMin FROM Ptj_Intrari_2 R WHERE YEAR(R.Ziua)= 2020 AND MONTH(R.Ziua)= 5 GROUP BY R.F10003) Q ON Q.F10003=A.F10003

                                LEFT JOIN Ptj_Contracte C on C.Id = Y.IdContract

                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "MP_NotaLichidare_Circuit" C ON B."IdSuper" = -1 * c."Supervizor"
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= AND B."DataInceput" <= '2020-06-15' AND '2020-06-15' <= B."DataSfarsit"
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "MP_NotaLichidare_Circuit" C ON C."Supervizor"=
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= AND B."DataInceput" <= '2020-06-15' AND '2020-06-15' <= B."DataSfarsit"
                        ) B

                            CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 900 THEN 'Candidat' ELSE CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 999 THEN 'Angajat in avans' ELSE (CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 0 THEN (CASE WHEN (A.F100925 <> 0 AND F100922 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100922 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100923 AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100924) THEN 'Activ suspendat' ELSE CASE WHEN (A.F100915 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= A.F100916) THEN 'Activ detasat' ELSE 'Activ' END END) ELSE 'Inactiv' END) END END AS "Stare",

                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10085,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Bloc. ' + a.F10085 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F100892,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Sc. ' + a.F100892 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F100893,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Et. ' + a.F100893 END) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100897 is null or a.F100897 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when niv3.tip in (11, 19, 22, 23) then ' sat ' + niv3.denloc else
                            case when niv3.tip = 6 and upper(niv3.denloc) not like '%SECTOR%' then ' sector ' + niv3.DENLOC else ' ' + niv3.denloc end END end) +

                            (case when a.F100914 is null or a.F100914 = 0 THEN '' else case when niv2.tip in (1, 4) and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' municipiul ' + niv2.DENLOC else
                            case when niv2.tip = 2 and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%ORAS%' then ' orasul ' + niv2.DENLOC else 
                            case when niv2.TIP = 3 and upper(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%COMUNA%' then ' comuna ' + niv2.DENLOC else ' ' + niv2.denloc end end end end ) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100921 is null or a.F100921 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%JUDET%' or upper(niv1.denloc)  like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' ' + niv1.DENLOC else
                             case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%BUCURESTI%' then ' municipiul ' + niv1.DENLOC else ' judetul ' + niv1.denloc end end END) +
                            

                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10087,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Cod Postal. ' + a.F10087 END) AS "AdresaCompleta"
                             F00810 as Birou
                            FROM F100 A
                            LEFT JOIN F002 E ON A.F10002 = E.F00202 
                            LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304 
                            LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405 
                            LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506 
                            LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607 
                            left join Localitati niv1 on niv1.SIRUTA = a.F100921
                            left join Localitati niv2 on niv2.SIRUTA = a.F100914
                            left join Localitati niv3 on niv3.SIRUTA = a.F100897
                             left join f008 on f100959=f00809  left join (select * from F100Supervizori where idsuper=3) as HR on HR.f10003=a.f10003
                            WHERE 1=1  AND A.F10003 IN (SELECT CAST(F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM USERS WHERE F70102 = 3
                            UNION
                            SELECT B.F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE C."IdSuper" = 3  AND ( e.F10025 = 0  OR  e.F10025 = 999 )
                            UNION
                            SELECT CAST(B.F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                            INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" D ON B.F10003=D.F10003 AND C."IdSuper" = -1 * D."IdSuper"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE D."IdUser" = 3  AND ( e.F10025 = 0  OR  e.F10025 = 999 ))
                            ) X WHERE 1=1  AND ( "Stare"='Activ' OR  "Stare"='Angajat in avans')
                            ORDER BY "NumeComplet"

                            CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 900 THEN '#ffff8000' ELSE CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 999 THEN '#dc96dc' ELSE (CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 0 THEN (CASE WHEN (A.F100925 <> 0 AND F100922 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100922 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100923 AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100924) THEN '#ffffffc8' ELSE CASE WHEN (A.F100915 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= A.F100916) THEN '#FF0066FF' ELSE '#ffc8ffc8' END END) ELSE '#ffffc8c8' END) END END AS "Culoare",
                            CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 900 THEN 'Candidat' ELSE CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 999 THEN 'Angajat in avans' ELSE (CASE WHEN A.F10025 = 0 THEN (CASE WHEN (A.F100925 <> 0 AND F100922 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100923 IS NOT NULL AND F100922 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100923 AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= F100924) THEN 'Activ suspendat' ELSE CASE WHEN (A.F100915 <= cast(getdate() as date)  AND cast(getdate() as date)  <= A.F100916) THEN 'Activ detasat' ELSE 'Activ' END END) ELSE 'Inactiv' END) END END AS "Stare",
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10083,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Str. ' + a.F10083 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10084,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Nr. ' + a.F10084 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10085,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Bloc. ' + a.F10085 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F100892,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Sc. ' + a.F100892 END) +
                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F100893,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Et. ' + a.F100893 END) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100897 is null or a.F100897 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when niv3.tip in (11, 19, 22, 23) then ' sat ' + niv3.denloc else
                            case when niv3.tip = 6 and upper(niv3.denloc) not like '%SECTOR%' then ' sector ' + niv3.DENLOC else ' ' + niv3.denloc end END end) +

                            (case when a.F100914 is null or a.F100914 = 0 THEN '' else case when niv2.tip in (1, 4) and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' municipiul ' + niv2.DENLOC else
                            case when niv2.tip = 2 and UPPER(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%ORAS%' then ' orasul ' + niv2.DENLOC else 
                            case when niv2.TIP = 3 and upper(niv2.DENLOC) not like '%COMUNA%' then ' comuna ' + niv2.DENLOC else ' ' + niv2.denloc end end end end ) +

                            (CASE WHEN a.F100921 is null or a.F100921 = 0 THEN '' ELSE case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%JUDET%' or upper(niv1.denloc)  like '%MUNICIPIU%' then ' ' + niv1.DENLOC else
                             case when upper(niv1.denloc) like '%BUCURESTI%' then ' municipiul ' + niv1.DENLOC else ' judetul ' + niv1.denloc end end END) +
                            

                            (CASE WHEN COALESCE(A.F10087,'') = '' THEN '' ELSE ' Cod Postal. ' + a.F10087 END) AS "AdresaCompleta"
                             , F00810 as Birou
                            FROM F100 A
                            LEFT JOIN F002 E ON A.F10002 = E.F00202 
                            LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304 
                            LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405 
                            LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506 
                            LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607 
                            left join Localitati niv1 on niv1.SIRUTA = a.F100921
                            left join Localitati niv2 on niv2.SIRUTA = a.F100914
                            left join Localitati niv3 on niv3.SIRUTA = a.F100897
                             , left join f1001 on a.f10003 = f1001.f10003 left join f008 on f100959=f00809  left join (select * from F100Supervizori where idsuper=3) as HR on HR.f10003=a.f10003
                            WHERE 1=1  AND A.F10003 IN (SELECT CAST(F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM USERS WHERE F70102 = 3
                            UNION
                            SELECT B.F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE C."IdSuper" = 3  AND ( e.F10025 = 0  OR  e.F10025 = 999 )
                            UNION
                            SELECT CAST(B.F10003 AS INT) AS F10003 FROM "relGrupAngajat" B
                            INNER JOIN "MP_relGrupSuper" C ON B."IdGrup" = C."IdGrup"
                            INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" D ON B.F10003=D.F10003 AND C."IdSuper" = -1 * D."IdSuper"
                             inner join f100 e on b.F10003=e.F10003 
                            WHERE D."IdUser" = 3  AND ( e.F10025 = 0  OR  e.F10025 = 999 ))
                            ) X WHERE 1=1  AND ( "Stare"='Activ' OR  "Stare"='Angajat in avans')
                            ORDER BY "NumeComplet"

Eroarea:   SELECT a.* FROM "MP_NotaLichidare_Detalii" a LEFT JOIN "MP_NotaLichidare" b on a."IdNotaLichidare" = b."IdAuto"  WHERE 1=1  AND F10003 IN (SELECT F10003 FROM (SELECT  A.F10003, A.F10008 + ' ' + A.F10009 AS "NumeComplet" 
                          FROM (
                        SELECT A.F10003
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = 4636 AND (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM "MP_NotaLichidare_Circuit" WHERE "Supervizor"=0) > 0
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "MP_NotaLichidare_Circuit" C ON B."IdSuper" = -1 * c."Supervizor"
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"=4636 AND B."DataInceput" <= '2020-06-17' AND '2020-06-17' <= B."DataSfarsit"
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        INNER JOIN "MP_NotaLichidare_Circuit" C ON C."Supervizor"=4636
                        WHERE B."IdUser"=4636 AND B."DataInceput" <= '2020-06-17' AND '2020-06-17' <= B."DataSfarsit"
                        ) B
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F002 C ON A.F10002 = C.F00202
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
                        LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506
                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607
						WHERE A.F10025 IN (0, 999) ) a)
